                <div class="pop-out Op-0" style="content:;position:absolute;border-style:solid;border-top-width:0;border-bottom-width:9px;border-left-width:8px;border-right-width:8px;border-color:#e7e7e7 transparent;display:block;height:0;width:0;z-index:2147483646;top:29px;left:50%;margin-left:-8px;transition-property:opacity;transition-duration:0.1s;transition-timing-function:linear;pointer-events:none;">
                </div>
                <div class="pop-out Op-0" style="position:absolute;overflow:hidden;margin-top:-3px;margin-left:-28.5px;top:40px;left:50%;right:;display:inline-block;transition-property:opacity;transition-duration:0.1s;transition-timing-function:linear;pointer-events:none;">
                 <div style="position:relative;background-color:white;-webkit-border-radius:5px;-moz-border-radius:5px;-khtml-border-radius:5px;border-radius:5px;border:solid 1px #e7e7e7;padding:4px;z-index:2147483645;">
                  <div style="width:47px;height:20px;">
                   <iframe allowtransparency="true" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" src="//www.facebook.com/plugins/like.php?href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2FYahooTravel&amp;width=47&amp;layout=button&amp;action=like&amp;show_faces=false&amp;share=false&amp;height=20" style="border:none;overflow:hidden;width:47px;height:35px;">
                   </iframe>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="Pos-r D-ib Cur-d Va-t" style="height:40px;">
               <div class="D-ib" style="height:40px;padding:0 11.5px;">
                <a class="D-ib" href="https://www.twitter.com/YahooTravel" rel="me" target="_blank">
                 <i class="Icon Fw-n Va-t" style="color:#00aceb;height:40px;line-height:40px;font-size:16px;">
                  
                 </i>
                </a>
                <div class="pop-out Op-0" style="content:;position:absolute;border-style:solid;border-top-width:0;border-bottom-width:8px;border-left-width:7px;border-right-width:7px;border-color:white transparent;display:block;height:0;width:0;z-index:2147483647;top:30px;left:50%;margin-left:-7px;transition-property:opacity;transition-duration:0.1s;transition-timing-function:linear;pointer-events:none;">
                </div>
                <div class="pop-out Op-0" style="content:;position:absolute;border-style:solid;border-top-width:0;border-bottom-width:9px;border-left-width:8px;border-right-width:8px;border-color:#e7e7e7 transparent;display:block;height:0;width:0;z-index:2147483646;top:29px;left:50%;margin-left:-8px;transition-property:opacity;transition-duration:0.1s;transition-timing-function:linear;pointer-events:none;">
                </div>
                <div class="pop-out Op-0" style="position:absolute;overflow:hidden;margin-top:-3px;margin-left:-35px;top:40px;left:50%;right:;display:inline-block;transition-property:opacity;transition-duration:0.1s;transition-timing-function:linear;pointer-events:none;">
                 <div style="position:relative;background-color:white;-webkit-border-radius:5px;-moz-border-radius:5px;-khtml-border-radius:5px;border-radius:5px;border:solid 1px #e7e7e7;padding:4px;z-index:2147483645;">

                 <div style="position:relative;background-color:white;-webkit-border-radius:5px;-moz-border-radius:5px;-khtml-border-radius:5px;border-radius:5px;border:solid 1px #e7e7e7;padding:4px;z-index:2147483645;">

            <div class="article-inner-container" style="max-width:1280px;">
             <div class="inset-container Mx-a">
              <div class="GridTable">
               <div class="D-tbr row-template">
                <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left">

                   <div class="D-tbr row-content">
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left Pend-20" style="width:305px;max-width:305px;">
                     <h1 class="Font-A-6-110 title W-100" id="article-aft-title-94092789892">
                      The Top 10 Zoos in the US Might Surprise You
                     </h1>
                     <div class="attribution-component D-b W-100" id="article-aft-attribution-94092789892" style="max-width:305px;">
                      <div class="author-info author-info-text-first Pt-10 W-100 Bd-t Bd-b Bdstart-0 Bdend-0">
                       <div class="GridTable W-100">
                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t">
                          <cite class="D-b Fs-n Pb-14 byline col">
                           <span class="D-b author-name col-left">
                            <a class="Font-C-2-140 Fw-b" data-action-outcome="navigate" data-routable-url="/travel/author/jo-piazza" data-ylk="t1:a2;t2:article;t3:cat;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:16;elm:itm;elmt:cat;itc:0" href="/travel/author/jo-piazza" rel="author" style="color:#000;">
                             Jo Piazza
                            </a>
                           </span>
                           <span class="D-b Font-C-2-140 Fw-n author-title">
                            Managing Editor
                           </span>
                           <time class="D-b Font-C-2-140 Fw-n date">
                            <span>
                             August 7, 2014
                            </span>
                           </time>
                           <div class="follow Mt-4">
                            <iframe allowtransparency="true" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" src="//platform.twitter.com/widgets/follow_button.html?screen_name=jopiazza&amp;show_screen_name=false&amp;show_count=false" style="border:none;overflow:hidden;width:60px;height:20px;">
                            </iframe>
                           </div>
                          </cite>
                         </div>
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t Va-b" style="width:133px;">
                          <a class="attribution-photo author-photo-link col" data-action-outcome="navigate" data-routable-url="/travel/author/jo-piazza" data-ylk="t1:a2;t2:article;t3:cat;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:16;elm:itm;elmt:cat;itc:0" href="/travel/author/jo-piazza">
                           <img alt="Jo Piazza" class="author-photo" src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w133/28facac3bebf145332caa007747eb0c4be75e950.png" style="width:133px;"/>
                          </a>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-right" style="max-width:500px;">
                     <div class="text-body-wrapper W-100 Font-B-1-160">
                      <noscript>
                      </noscript>
                      <div class="text-body W-100 Font-B-1-160" id="article-aft-text-body-94092789892" style="color:#222222;max-width:500px;">
                       <div class="body read-more-cut">
                        <div class="pre-cut" style="height:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;">
                         <p>
                          Here at Yahoo Travel we occasionally travel for the animals. Weve been to China
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://www.yahoo.com/travel/we-here-at-yahoo-travel-like-to-get-up-close-and-85839849332.html" target="_blank">
                           to cuddle a baby panda
                          </a>
                          , Australia to have quality time with a koala and Africa to meet the
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://www.yahoo.com/travel/watch-saving-a-hedgehog-from-bamakos-death-93890184527.html" target="_blank">
                           worlds most adorable hedgehog
                          </a>
                          .
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          But you dont need to leave the country to do some creature peeping of your own. Why not head to San Diego to see a panda, or feed a giraffe in Memphis or see a baby leopard cub in Denver.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          According to data mined from
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/PressCenter-i6885-c1-Press_Releases.html" target="_blank">
                           TripAdvisors
                          </a>
                          community of millions of users, these are the very best zoos right here in our own backyard.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Related:
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://yhoo.it/1iKsEwg" target="_blank">
                             Please DO Feed the Animals Here
                            </a>
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="The Top 10 Zoos in the US Might Surprise You" height="383" src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/b5113cb53f2b70a1442407cf130e2d1a70c86ce0.jpg" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           In Omaha, you can wave hello to this little guy. (Photo: Henry Doorly Zoo)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           1.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.omahazoo.com/" target="_blank">
                            Henry Doorly Zoo
                           </a>
                           , Omaha, Nebraska
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Head to Gorilla Valley, Orangutang Forest or Stingray beach at one of the largest and most interactive zoos in America.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/99e4def965c6ea22b81c2183a16478e73055dc1b.jpg" height="321" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           You dont have to go all the way to China to see a panda. (Photo: TripAdvisor)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           2.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://zoo.sandiegozoo.org/" target="_blank">
                            San Diego Zoo
                           </a>
                           , San Diego, California
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          The San Diego Zoo lets you do early morning tours with the pandas or late nights with the koalas. Take your pick. But dont take our word for it. You can check it out for yourself with one of their
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://zoo.sandiegozoo.org/" target="_blank">
                           many live animals cameras
                          </a>
                          .
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Watch This Baby Panda Turn 2!
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <iframe data-src="https://screen.yahoo.com/precious-san-diego-zoo-panda-152556030.html?format=embed&amp;player_autoplay=false" height="393.75" width="700">
                          </iframe>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/b9047f27233f11ad32544ba1ad31260567414964.jpg" height="333" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           Get your groove on while the elephants cool off at the St. Louis Zoo. (Photo: TripAdvisor)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                        </div>
                        <div class="post-cut W-100" id="post-cut" style="transition-property:none;-webkit-transition-property:none;transition-duration:10s;-webkit-transition-duration:10s;transition-timing-function:ease-in;-webkit-transition-timing-function:ease-in;overflow:hidden;max-height:0;max-width:500px;">
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           3.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.stlzoo.org/events/calendarofevents/jungleboogie/" target="_blank">
                            St. Louis Zoo
                           </a>
                           , Saint Louis, Missouri
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          This zoo cranks up their rock and roar every weekend with their Jungle Boogie concert series, where admission to the zoo and the concert are both free.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Related:
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://yhoo.it/1mv3t2X" target="_blank">
                             The Cutest Baby Animals You Will See on Safari
                            </a>
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/9c643cc7fba6749991d60a6a72567df77fe3b6c6.jpg" height="375" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           And you thought you had to go to Africa to get this close to the rhinos. (Photo: TripAdvisor)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           4.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.sdzsafaripark.org/" target="_blank">
                            San Diego Zoo Safari Park
                           </a>
                           , Escondido, California
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          The city of San Diego has gone and gotten a twofer when it comes to incredible zoos. Join the Africa Tram here or the Lemur Walk. Witness the fastest land mammal, the cheetah, up close and personal as it goes for a run. Fancy getting above it all? Get a birds eye view in the Balloon Safari high above the park.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/11a94e1f19191b89926a51aa1a90fd4b5dcef05b.jpg" height="388" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           The giraffes here just want to get to know you better. (Photo: TripAdvisor)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           5.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://cmzoo.org/" target="_blank">
                            Cheyenne Mountain Zoo
                           </a>
                           , Colorado Springs, Colorado
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Set on146 acres with 550 animals from 119 species, this charming Rocky Mountain zoo lets you ride above the animals in a refurbished chairlift.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/e79b7ac920fcdecc134787f5017cb5a75d15884e.jpg" height="375" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           This guy looks ready for a nap. (Photo: TripAdvisor)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           6.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://memphiszoo.org/" target="_blank">
                            Memphis Zoo
                           </a>
                           , Memphis, Tennessee
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Forget Graceland. Head to the Memphis Zoo, where you can feed the penguins, giraffes, and the elephants.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            Related:
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://yhoo.it/1tIt0xt" target="_blank">
                             The Fascinating Animals You Will Meet on Kangaroo Island
                            </a>
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/4fcb86dd2af20d0f37a76e267fa3ead9638fdc8a.jpg" height="316" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           Meet Saya, the clouded baby leopard cub. (Photo: Denver Zoo)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           7.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g33388-d128664-Reviews-Denver_Zoo-Denver_Colorado.htmlhttp://denverzoo.org/events/17th-annual-brew-zoo" target="_blank">
                            Denver Zoo
                           </a>
                           , Denver, Colorado
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Go right now and you wont just see the zoos three cuddly wolf cubs, but youll get to see the three clouded leopard cubs. Hurry. They grow up fast. Its most fun to head there during one of their special events like the ice cream social or Brew at the Zoo, which features tastings from 40 local breweries.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/443b41d40c66b74a58361c57ba2f1443ce6736a8.jpg" height="667" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           You dont go to the parrots, they come to you here. (Photo: TripAdvisor)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           8.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.riverbanks.org/" target="_blank">
                            Riverbanks Zoos and Botanical Garden
                           </a>
                           , Columbia, South Carolina
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Its good now  but its about to be better. Riverbanks just broke ground on a $36-million expansion and development project that will create astate-of-the-art seal/sea lion exhibit, a new grizzly bear, and an otter habitat.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/9cc1399fa8c3084c306a9af9d0f9af4777cabb3b.jpg" height="375" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="500"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           And you thought youd have to go to Rajasthan to see a tiger this close. (Photo: TripAdvisor)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           9.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.zoomiami.org/Daily%20Activites" target="_blank">
                            Zoo Miami
                           </a>
                           , Miami, Florida
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          You havent really lived until youve fed a one-horned Indian rhino out of the palm of your hand. This is the place to cross that off your bucket list.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <img alt="image" data-src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w483/f72e0bbc3489c79d3885c60943339b99c1275ec1.jpg" height="329" src="https://s.yimg.com/g/images/spaceball.gif" width="483"/>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <em>
                           Bowie the baby elephant just turned one! (Photo: Fort Worth Zoo Facebook)
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           10.
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:af6e93a6-77cb-3838-a1fb-660c7ea1bdbc;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.fortworthzoo.org/about-us/history/" target="_blank">
                            Fort Worth Zoo
                           </a>
                           , Fort Worth, Texas
                          </strong>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Pay a visit to the oldest zoo in Texas. Back in 1909 the zoo had just one lion, two bear cubs, an alligator, a coyote and a few rabbits. Today they have more than 7,000 animals. Thats what we call a growth spurt.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <b>
                           WATCH: Spend the Best Day of Your Life in an Animal Retirement Home.
                          </b>
                         </p>

                         </p>

                         Daydream
                        </a>
                       </div>

                        <span class="item-title Font-A-3-120 D-b" style="word-wrap:break-word;margin-left:175px;">
                         #Daydream: Rialto Beach inOlympic National Park, Washington
                        </span>

(Courtesy Ski Portillo\u002FFacebook)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EMeanwhile, \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.vallenevado.com\u002Fen\u002F\"\u003EValle Nevado Ski Resort\u003C\u002Fa\u003E in Chile boasted photos on its Facebook page Monday reporting 31 inches of snow over the weekend. The full resort is set to open July 17, but Valle Nevado says it may have enough snow to open for day skiers by Wednesday.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThis could help salvage a tough year for skiing in which resorts in the western U.S. closed early after receiving less than half their normal snowfall. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EA mild El Ni&#xF1;o was reported in May by the National Oceanic and Atmospheric Association, with predictions but no guarantee it would gain strength later, which it failed to do last year despite similar optimism. If this storm fulfills its promise, there&#x2019;s a 70 percent chance of lasting through September and a 60 percent chance of lasting through December. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETo follow the latest snow reports by ski resort, you can visit \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.j2ski.com\u002F\"\u003EJ2ski.com\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWATCH:&#xA0; \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Favalanches-death-threats-and-no-lifts-welcome-to-101875241912.html\"\u003EAvalanches, Death Threats, and No Lifts. The Walt Disney Co. is getting the break because they intend to spend the money on a $1 billion expansion of their parks in Anaheim. This makeover will not only lead to new attractions, it will also mean more jobs for the people of Anaheim.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EDisney is already the biggest employer in the city, providing 28,000 jobs for those in surrounding communities. HeresHow Not to Make a Fool of Yourself","summary":"If you want to keep your job, we suggest you read on and take notes.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F0a81f1e965a02fa22fbf86c49f5e4d56427af105.gif\" alt=\"Traveling With Your Boss? Here&#x2019;s&#xA0;How Not to Make a Fool of Yourself\" width=\"540\" height=\"766\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EIllustration by Erik Mace\u002FYahoo\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThere&#x2019;s a business trip on the calendar, and you&#x2019;re traveling with your boss. While it might seem like common sense, there are some very simple dos and don&#x2019;ts of to remember when you&#x2019;re traveling with your superior. If you want to keep your job, we suggest you read on and take notes.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EDon&#x2019;t pack like you&#x2019;re going on vacation\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F3660b6618760b55cfb20418ee69c36ca9f38b71b.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EAppropriately dressed woman on work trip. &#xA0;(Photo: Thinkstock)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ETranslation: Leave the Herve Leger dresses, short shorts, and sheer blouses at home. Regardless of where your work trip takes you&#x2014;New York City, Jamaica or Miami&#x2014; this is not the time to show some skin, bare your cleavage or prove just how toned SoulCycle has made your legs. The rule is simple: If you wouldn&#x2019;t wear it to work, don&#x2019;t wear it on a work trip. Office-appropriate dress codes still apply. Should your job take you somewhere warm (who among us has been able to avoid the Las Vegas Convention Center), make sure to pack light fabrics that breathe as opposed to slinky ones that make others breathe heavy&#x2014;it&#x2019;s an important differentiation.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Ftake-a-bizcation-96120868057.html\"\u003EThe Bizcation: The Ultimate Way to Enjoy Business Travel\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EJust say no to the in-flight service-slash-mini bar-slash-lobby bar\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fb8a8ff8c2d10d4a58a3309b0a82d2e594e48e27a.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ETiny liquor bottles on ice (Photo: Thinkstock)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EWe get it, the jingle of tiny bottles on the flight attendant&#x2019;s cart as it passes by you on a long plane trip is tempting. Or the way the miniature versions of your favorite liquor are arranged so beautifully in your room&#x2019;s mini bar. Or how that beautiful, deep mahogany lobby bar seems to be calling your name, asking you to sit down and stay a while. Just. Say. No.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EGetting drunk or even buzzed can lead to awkward moments when spending off-duty hours with your boss. This is not the time to get sloppy and explain to him\u002Fher that you really do deserve that promotion\u002Fraise\u002Fcorner office. That&#x2019;s not to say you can&#x2019;t have a drink with dinner&#x2014;being a straightedge isn&#x2019;t necessarily good either&#x2014;but know your limit and stay South of it. Like Deep South of it. &#xA0; \u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EKeep the conversation topics bland and water-cooler appropriate.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"355\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fd0815c7beea6506bea9ca3a34c162c583753a6d0.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EKeep conversation work friendly (Photo: Thinkstock)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EI&#x2019;m sorry you&#x2019;re getting divorced, but just because we boarded a plane together doesn&#x2019;t mean I want to hear about it. This is not the time to bare your soul to your boss. If you wouldn&#x2019;t casually say it while small talking in the office hallway then don&#x2019;t say it now. &#xA0;It may \u003Ci\u003Efeel\u003C\u002Fi\u003E like personal time given that you are out of the office&#x2014;perhaps spending a lot of time together in the airport or hotel&#x2014;but that doesn&#x2019;t mean confessing all your private affairs is a good idea. Your boss likely does not want to hear about your ne&#x2019;er-do-well brother, complicated finances, weird rash, nasty divorce, or last Tinder date. Not only does it cross into some uncomfortable gray area, it could perhaps work against you later should they be one of the loose-lipped variety. Keep your personal business just that&#x2014;personal.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EStop calling\u002Ftexting your significant other\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"380\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F0ef53769808b0859321453009d2426f84bf47fa1.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EKeep texts to your &#xA0;girlfriend\u002Fboyfriend\u002Fhusband\u002Fwife to a minimum (Photo: ThinkStock)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EYou&#x2019;re on a work trip and miss your girlfriend\u002Fboyfriend\u002Fhusband\u002Fwife. That does not give you permission to spend half the trip on your phone, texting flirty messages, endless emojis, and selfie after selfie of you in front of the [fill in recognizable landmark here]. Check in with him\u002Fher from the privacy of your own hotel room at the beginning of the day and again at the end if necessary. Constant communication&#x2014;especially during a meeting or lecture&#x2014;is unprofessional, not to mention annoying for those around you. Your relationship should be able to withstand a few days apart. Remember, absence is supposed to make the heart grow fonder, not make you go over your data plan.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EThis is a work trip, not a dating app\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F4f162efe5e6aafac08acf3f527e7536a8c700323.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EStop flirting with the waiter\u002Fconcierge\u002Fguy at bar or&#x2014;gasp&#x2014;coworker.&#xA0;(Photo: Thickstock)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ESure, you&#x2019;re away from home and meeting new people you may or may not find attractive. Or perhaps you never noticed just how cute your coworker is (and he\u002Fshe is funny! Who knew?), but still, out-and-out flirting is a bad idea that can get you into trouble and send a message about you that you don&#x2019;t want communicated. Greenlands Finest Microbrew Beers","summary":"I'm a beer woman. So on my trip to Greenland, when I heard there was a craft brewery in town, I made a beeline for it.","body":"\u003Cp\u003EAnybody who knows me knows I don&#x2019;t drink vodka. I don&#x2019;t do tequila. And I&#x2019;ve never been a big fan of anything that comes with a garnish. I am, however, a beer girl. Raised in Cincinnati, a town with German roots, I have a deep love of hops, and over the years my tastes have been refined from \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fhudepohlbeer.com\u002F\"\u003EHudepohl\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and Schlitz to craft beers. Don&#x2019;t get me wrong &#x2014; when stuck on a riverboat for a bachelorette party in, say, Austin, Texas (thanks to my sister Emily), I will still happily down a Bud, a Coors, or a Schlitz. But I have learned to appreciate the fine craft of beer making and love a small-batch brew. So on my trip to Greenland, when I heard there was a craft brewery in town, I made a beeline for it.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Ffinger-pulling-head-pulling-and-kick-the-seal-122521580652.html\"\u003EFinger Pulling and Kick the Seal &#x2014; Welcome to the Arctic Games!\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F93fb6d09ed4cf36c50b1cd8100b9a9da95be5f9d.png\" alt=\"Taste-Testing Greenland&#x2019;s Finest Microbrew Beers\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThe Godthaab Bryghus brewery is in a building that conveniently also houses a dive bar called Daddy&#x2019;s. While &#x201C;Daddy&#x201D; is a great guy named Gert, the actual brewery is run by Mikael Sorenson, who swears that the beer there is made with glacier ice that is at least 2,000 years old.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Yes, we have men who go out onto the ice and cut slabs off the glaciers for us and bring them back here for our beer,&#x201D; Sorenson said.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E[Side note: Apparently ice cutting is a big business. Down the street is an ice cream shop that also uses 2,000-year-old ice. &#x201C;Ice cream in Greenland?&#x201D; you may be asking. &#x201C;Isn&#x2019;t it cold enough?&#x201D; No. It&#x2019;s not. Greenland has the second largest ice cream consumption per capita in the world, second only to Finland. Go figure.]\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F3a590de53797cb2f646953e3212a190735cb2dff.png\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EWhile there are no official stats on how much beer is consumed in &#xA0;Nuuk, Greenland&#x2019;s capital, judging by the crowds in the bars and the continual snow, I&#x2019;d say it ranks right up there. And frankly, I can&#x2019;t say I blame them &#x2014; the weather is rough (see previous episode: &#x201C;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fsnowmageddon-2015-cabin-fever-hits-hard-in-123462240287.html\"\u003ESnowmageddon 2015: Cabin Fever Hits Hard in Greenland\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#x201D;), and the beer is delicious. At the time I visited, there were five beers on tap, including the Musk Ox, the Eric the Red, and the Polar Bear (they like to name the beers after local animals). And here&#x2019;s a tip: While they are all delicious, if you ever find yourself at Daddy&#x2019;s in Nuuk, ask for Gert and Mikael and get them to give you the unfiltered versions of all the beers. They may smell like dirty feet, but they taste like heaven.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fsnowmageddon-2015-cabin-fever-hits-hard-in-123462240287.html\"\u003ESnowmageddon 2015: Cabin Fever Hits Hard in Greenland\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThere is only one problem with the Godthaab Bryghus beer &#x2014; while it is possibly the best beer I have ever tasted (and trust: I have tasted a lot of beer), they don&#x2019;t export. So to get 2,000-year-old glacier-water beer, you have to go to the source. It&#x2019;s worth it. \u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day.
